Notation:
- Roots of cycles are denoted by b_0, b_1, .. b_(period-1) and are taken to be distinct.
- Elementary symmetric functions are denoted by capital letters A (sum b_i), B (sum b_i*b_k with i <> k) etc).
- The seed in the iteration z^2+c is denoted by the lowcase letter 'c'.

- simplifcation of equation involve dividing by the greatest common divisor and reducing the degree of
  the seed if it occurs in all terms.



1) For equation 1, construct the following function and first express
it in elementary symmetric functions as is [2] and secondly, apply
the iterational relationship (b_(i+1 mod 67)-c)^n=b_i^2n
as often as possible express it as far as possible byelementary symmetric functions
and equate both expressions to arrive at the final equation.

  sum [ b_i0^2]
    for indices 0 <= i0 <= 6

which gives

  +1*A^2+-2*B
    =
  +1*A+-7*c

  eq[id=1] +1*A^2+-2*B+-1*A++7*c = 0


2) For equation 2, construct the following function and express it.
in two ways as above.

  sum [ b_i0^2*b_i1^2]
    for indices 0 <= i0 <> i1 <= 6

which gives

  +2*B^2+-4*A*C++4*D
    =
  +2*B+-12*c*A++42*c^2

  eq[id=2] +1*B^2+-2*A*C++2*D+-1*B++6*c*A+-21*c^2 = 0


3) For equation 3, construct the following function and express it.
in two ways as above.

  sum [ b_i0^2*b_i1^2*b_i2^2]
    for indices 0 <= i0 <> i1 <> i2 <= 6

which gives

  +6*C^2+-12*B*D++12*A*E+-12*F
    =
  +6*C+-30*c*B++90*c^2*A+-210*c^3

  eq[id=3] +1*C^2+-2*B*D++2*A*E+-2*F+-1*C++5*c*B+-15*c^2*A++35*c^3 = 0


4) For equation 4, construct the following function and express it.
in two ways as above.

  sum [ b_i0^2*b_i1^2*b_i2^2*b_i3^2]
    for indices 0 <= i0 <> i1 <> i2 <> i3 <= 6

which gives

  +24*D^2+-48*C*E++48*B*F+-48*A*G
    =
  +24*D+-96*c*C++240*c^2*B+-480*c^3*A++840*c^4

  eq[id=4] +1*D^2+-2*C*E++2*B*F+-2*A*G+-1*D++4*c*C+-10*c^2*B++20*c^3*A+-35*c^4 = 0


7) For equation 7, construct the following function and express it.
in two ways as above.

  sum [ b_i0^2*b_i1^2*b_i2^2*b_i3^2*b_i4^2*b_i5^2*b_i6^2]
    for indices 0 <= i0 <> i1 <> i2 <> i3 <> i4 <> i5 <> i6 <= 6

which gives

  +5040*G^2
    =
  +5040*G+-5040*c*F++5040*c^2*E+-5040*c^3*D++5040*c^4*C+-5040*c^5*B++5040*c^6*A+-5040*c^7

  eq[id=7] +1*G^2+-1*G++1*c*F+-1*c^2*E++1*c^3*D+-1*c^4*C++1*c^5*B+-1*c^6*A++1*c^7 = 0

12) Equation 12 is based on a binomial reduction of the cyclic function

  6
  PROD [ b_k^2 - b_(k+delta mod p)^2) ]
  k=0

with delta=1 in this case and which can be expressed in two ways

  PROD [ (b_k+b_(k+delta mod p))*(b_k - b_(k+delta mod p)) ]

and on the other hand after using the iterational relatiionship b_k^2=b_(k+1 mod p)-c
to lower the degrees

  PROD [ b_(k+1 mod p)-c - b_(k+delta+1 mod p) + c ]

which equals as a cyclic function PROD (b_k-b_(k+delta mod p)

Hence both sides can be divided by the same product which results in

  1 = PROD [ b_k + b_(k+delta mod p) ]

This equation is then multiplied by the cyclic function

  6
  SUM b_(k+0 mod p)^2
  0 <= k <= 6

Powers of roots are reduced by the iterational relation and the
equation is expressed in elementary symmetric functions as far as possible, which leads to

[id=12] -1*G++2*c*G+-1*F++3*c*F+-2*c^2*E+-1*E++4*c*E+-1*D++5*c*D+-5*c^2*D+-1*C+-9*c^2*C++2*c^3*C++6*c*C+-1*B++7*c^3*B++7*c*B+-14*c^2*B+-1*A++8*c*A+-2*c^4*A+-20*c^2*A++16*c^3*A+-9*c^4++30*c^3+-27*c^2++7*c = 0

13) Equation 13 is based on a binomial reduction of the cyclic function

  6
  PROD [ b_k^2 - b_(k+delta mod p)^2) ]
  k=0

with delta=1 in this case and which can be expressed in two ways

  PROD [ (b_k+b_(k+delta mod p))*(b_k - b_(k+delta mod p)) ]

and on the other hand after using the iterational relatiionship b_k^2=b_(k+1 mod p)-c
to lower the degrees

  PROD [ b_(k+1 mod p)-c - b_(k+delta+1 mod p) + c ]

which equals as a cyclic function PROD (b_k-b_(k+delta mod p)

Hence both sides can be divided by the same product which results in

  1 = PROD [ b_k + b_(k+delta mod p) ]

This equation is then multiplied by the cyclic function

  6
  SUM b_(k+0 mod p)^3
  0 <= k <= 6

Powers of roots are reduced by the iterational relation and the
equation is expressed in elementary symmetric functions as far as possible, which leads to

[id=13] -1*G++3*c*G+-1*F+-2*c^2*F++4*c*F+-1*E+-5*c^2*E++5*c*E+-1*D++2*c^3*D++6*c*D+-9*c^2*D+-1*C++7*c*C++7*c^3*C+-14*c^2*C+-1*B+-20*c^2*B++16*c^3*B+-2*c^4*B++8*c*B+-27*c^2*A++9*c*A+-1*A++30*c^3*A+-9*c^4*A+-35*c^2++7*c++2*c^5++50*c^3+-25*c^4 = 0


--) Equation 1 is solved for symbol B which leads to

  B = ( -1*A^2++1*A+-7*c) / (-2)

700) Equation 700 is directly set to

[id=700] +4*c+-1 = 0


701) Equation 701 is directly set to

[id=701] +2*c^2+-3*c*A+-4*c++1*A++1 = 0


900) For Equation 900, the following operation is performed

  eq513*(+1  )
    / (if remainder-free and right equations sides are 0)
  [eq700*(+1)]^1

    / (if remainder-free and right equations sides are 0)
  [eq1202*(+1)]^6

which leads (after possible simplification) to

^5++3060*G^4+-816*G^3++153*G^2+-18*G++1 = 0

For a given seed c, the equation results in a polynomial only in G.
That polynomial's G-degree of 18 equals the maximum number of cycles of length 7.

The hyperbolic centers of exact period 7 are described by

+1*c^63++32*c^62++496*c^61++4976*c^60++36440*c^59++208336*c^58++971272*c^57++3807704*c^56++12843980*c^55++37945904*c^54++99582920*c^53++234813592*c^52++502196500*c^51++981900168*c^50++1766948340*c^49++2943492972*c^48++4562339774*c^47++6609143792*c^46++8984070856*c^45++11500901864*c^44++13910043524*c^43++15941684776*c^42++17357937708*c^41++17999433372*c^40++17813777994*c^39++16859410792*c^38++15286065700*c^37++13299362332*c^36++11120136162*c^35++8948546308*c^34++6939692682*c^33++5193067630*c^32++3754272037*c^31++2625062128*c^30++1777171560*c^29++1166067016*c^28++742179284*c^27++458591432*c^26++275276716*c^25++160617860*c^24++91143114*c^23++50323496*c^22++27049196*c^21++14162220*c^20++7228014*c^19++3598964*c^18++1749654*c^17++831014*c^16++385741*c^15++175048*c^14++77684*c^13++33708*c^12++14290*c^11++5916*c^10++2398*c^9++950*c^8++365*c^7++132*c^6++42*c^5++14*c^4++5*c^3++2*c^2++1*c++1

which equals the coefficient of the G^0-term, i.e. after setting the
product of periodic points G to 0 (= superattracting).


Final: The system consists of equations 1600
where all right hand sides = 0 
in the variables G, c
